Aadi 8, Visuvaavasu, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2056
GREATER CHENNAI CORPORATION CHENNAI - 600 003.
NORMS FOR THE STREET VENDORS & LIST OF DECLARED VENDING ZONES  
AND NON VENDING ZONES 
	
	
	
	
            (R.D.C.No.SUSV/3415-10/2023)	
No. SRO C-30(a)/2025.
The following norms applicable to street vendors has been determined in accordance with Section 21 of the Street 
Vendors (Protection of Livelihoods and Regulation of Street Vending) Act, 2014:- 
“21. Plan for street vending:- 	
(1) Every local authority shall, in consultation with the planning authority and on the recommendations of the 
Town Vending Committee once in every five years, prepare a plan to promote the vocation of street 
vendors covering the matters contained in the First Schedule.
(2) The plan for street vending prepared by the local authority shall be submitted to the appropriate Government 
for approval and that Government shall, before notifying the plan, determine the norms applicable to the 
street vendors”.
The Town Vending Committee of the Greater Chennai Corporation recommended the Norms for street vendors and 
list of 150 Vending Zones and 188 Non Vending Zones for approval of the Council. Accordingly, Council approved 
and passed the Resolution vide No.525/2025 dated 30.04.2025. In continuation of the Resolution, the Government 
has published the Norms for Street Vendors vide G.O.(3ப), No.8 Municipal Administration and Water Supply (M.C.2) 
Department, dated 07.07.2025. 
As per the Certificate issued by the Municipal Administration and Water Supply (MC-2) Department, the Ordinary 
Gazette and Extraordinary Gazette are being issued for the Street Vendor Plans comprising the Norms for Street 
Vendors and list of 150 Vending Zones and 188 Non Vending Zones in respect of the Greater Chennai Corporation.


2	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
(1) The plan for street vending shall,— 
(a) 	 ensure that all existing street vendors identified in the survey, subject to a norm conforming to two and 
half percent of the population of the ward, zone, town or city, as the case may be, are accommodated 
in the plan for street vending;
(b) 	 ensure the right of commuters to move freely and use the roads without any impediment; 
(c) 	 ensure that the provision of space or area for street vending is reasonable and consistent with existing 
natural markets; 
(d) 	 take into account the civic facilities for appropriate use of identified spaces or areas as vending zones; 
(e) 	 promote convenient, efficient and cost effective distribution of goods and provision of services; 
(f) 	 such other matters as may be specified in the scheme to give effect to the plan for street vending.
(2) The plan for street vending shall contain all of the following matters, namely:— 
(a) determination of spatial planning norms for street vending; 
(b) earmarking of space or area for vending zones; 
(c) determination of vending zones as restriction-free-vending zones, restricted vending zones and no-vending 
zones; 
(d) making of spatial plans conducive and adequate for the prevalent number of street vendors in that city or 
town and also for the future growth, by adopting such norms as may be necessary; 
(e) consequential changes needed in the existing master plan, development plan, zonal plan, layout plan and 
any other plan for accommodating street vendors in the designated vending zones.
(3) Declaration of no-vending zone shall be carried out by the plan for street vending, subject to the following 
principles, namely:— 
(a) any existing market, or a natural market as identified under the survey shall not be declared as a 
no-vending zone; 
(b) declaration of no-vending zone shall be done in a manner which displaces the minimum percentage of 
street vendors; 
(c) overcrowding of any place shall not be a basis for declaring any area as a no-vending zone provided 
that restrictions may be placed on issuing certificate of vending in such areas to persons not identified 
as street vendors in the survey; 
(d) sanitary concerns shall not be the basis for declaring any area as a no-vending zone unless such concerns 
can be solely attributed to street vendors and cannot be resolved through appropriate civic action by 
the local authority; 
(e) till such time as the survey has not been carried out and the plan for street vending has not been 
formulated, no zone shall be declared as a no-vending zone.
A plan for street vending should be formulated according to the above guidelines:
 1) The area where the street vendors can be operated within the limits of the corporation, two and a half 
percent of the population of that area/ward may be allowed to operate,
(a) Section 3 (2) of the street vendors (Protection of Livelihood and Regulation of street vending ) Act, 2014
2) Hawking may not be permitted where, e.g. due to narrowness of road, free flow of traffic or movement 
of pedestrians is hindered or where for security reasons an area is required to be kept free or near 
hospitals, places of worship etc. 


	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY	
3
(b) Para No.7-10, of Supreme Court Order on Maharashtra Ekta Hawkwers Union & Anr vs Greater Municipal  
Corporation, dated 09.09.2013.
3) The Town Vending Committee should ensure that the provision of space for vendors’ markets are pragmatic, 
consistent with formation of natural markets, sufficient for existing demand for the street vendors’ goods and services 
as well as likely increase in accordance with anticipated population growth.
The Town Vending Committee should monitor the provision of civic facilities and their functioning in Vending Zones 
and Vendors’ Markets and bring shortcomings, if any to the notice of the concerned authorities of the urban local body. 
The TVC should also promote the organisation of weekly markets, festival bazaars, night bazaars, vending festivals 
on important holidays etc. as well as take up necessary improvement of infrastructure facilities and municipal services 
with the urban local body concerned.
(c) Para No.15-4.5.1 (b) and (c) of Supreme Court order on Maharashtra Ekta Hawkers Union & Anr vs 
Greater Municipal Corporation, dated 09.09.2013
	
4) Every street vendor shall maintain civic amenities and public property in the vending zone in good condition 
and not damage or destroy or cause any damage or destruction to the same. 
	
Every street vendor shall pay such periodic maintenance charges for the civic amenities and facilities provided 
in the vending zones as may be determined by the local authority. 
(d) Section 16 and 17 of the Street Vendors (Protection of Livelihood and Regulation of Street Vending) 
Act, 2014
The procedures to identity the vending zones:
 
 A place where sales can be made is a sidewalk, roadside area, public waiting area, and any other area or 
place where temporary business can be conducted on the sidewalk and recommended by the Town Vending 
Committee and approved by the government.
 
 The Town Vending Committee may declare places where part-time sales can be made at a specific time, on 
a specific day, in a specific week, in a specific month, and in a specific year.
 
 For other types of vendors, i.e., Street vendors who naturally trade in the weekly market, traditional market, 
festival market and seasonal market within their jurisdiction should be allowed to continue to trade by the 
Town Vending committee.
 
 Vending should not be allowed in private areas. At the same time, the Town Vending committee may allow 
the site of privately owned with the consent of the property owner while trying to remove street vendors from 
public places or provide them with alternative site.
 
 The police should be consulted in selecting the places where vending can be found in the areas within the 
jurisdiction of the police department and the traffic police department.
 
 	 A place for vending recommended by the Police Department or Traffic Police Department, the Corporation 
may, with due reasons, accept, amend or reject that place/area as a place where vending can be allowed.
 
 Street vending may be prohibited on roads with a minimum width of one meter with two-way traffic. However, 
if such roads are declared as prohibited for vehicular for any reason, street vending may be permitted. 
 
 Street vending should not be allowed on roads with a width of 3 meters to 5 meters. However, if such a 
road is declared as a one-way traffic, street vending may be allowed. 
 
 On wide roads with a width of 5 to 6 meters, street vending may be allowed on only one side.
 
 Street vending may be permitted on both sides of roads with a width of 10 meters and above.
 
 After determining the vending zones where street vending can be permitted, the Town Vending Committee 
may decide how many vendors are allowed to permit on such streets.
 
 Street vending may be permitted after obtaining permission from the Traffic Police to ensure that vehicles and 
pedestrians can pass without hindrance. If necessary, parking of vehicles in these areas may be prohibited.


4	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
The procedures for identifying non-vending zones:
 
 Vending prohibited areas are places not approved by the Town Vending Committee.
 
 Even if it is a place where there is a minimum percent vending causing inconvenience to the public and the 
local people, such places may be declared as places where vending is prohibited.
 
 As per the Railways Act 1989, Land and places owned and controlled by the Railways Department, the 
Street Vending Act does not apply.
 
 Street Vendors Act does not apply for the land and areas belongs to National and State Government Highways.
 
 Street vending shall not be allowed for the areas within 100 meters of places of worship, educational institutions 
and hospitals and the areas within 150 meters of other markets (markets) and railway stations.
 
Street Vending shall not be allowed within the area of 150 meters of the entrance and exit points of government 
buildings, high courts, other courts, district collectors’ offices and fire stations.
 
Street Vending shall not be allowed in the areas specified in the Ancient Monuments and Archaeological Sites 
and Remains Act, 2010 and the State Archaeological Monuments Protection Act.
 
Street Vending shall not be allowed in any area prohibited by the government for safety reasons.
Standard Operating Procedures (SOP) as mentioned in the Chief Engineer (General)’s circular vide C.E.(General) 
Na.Ka.No.A1/366/2024, dated 03.12.2024.
1. 	 The Town Vending Committee has declared as a 100-meter radius of educational institutions such as 
schools and colleges within the limits of the Greater Chennai Corporation as a prohibited area for street 
vending (No Vending Zone).
2. 	 The listed 22 streets as prohibited for parking as received from the Deputy Commissioner of Police 
(Traffic) have been declared as non-vending zones by the Town Vending Committee.
3. 	 The Town Vending Committee shall erect green colour notice boards in the area where street vending are 
permitted (Vending Zone) and red colour notice boards in the areas where street vending are prohibited 
(No Vending Zone).
4. 	 The size of notice boards shall be 2X1 (2 feet x 1 feet) and street names shall be written in Tamil and 
English.
5. 	 In all zones, the area of the street vending stall permitted by the Town Vending Committee to be set up in 
the Vending zone should be measured (earmarked) uniformly in green colour in size 6×4 (6 feet × 4 feet).
6. 	 The size of the street vending stalls to be set up in the vending zone should be 6×4 (6 feet × 4 feet) 
and the distance between two stalls should be 2’ (2 feet) in any size. The stalls should be measured 
(earmarked) excluding the path leading to commercial establishments, homes and offices located on the 
road and the width of the sidewalk should be ensured so that pedestrians can walk without allowing 
vehicles to park in front of the sidewalk stalls.
7. 	 The stall sizes can be earmarked after obtaining the approval of the standard commercial establishments 
already located along the road (or) the stalls can be measured excluding establishments that cannot 
obtain approval.

பெெருநகர செென்னை மாநகராாட்சி, செென்னை – 600 003
பெெருநகர செென்னை மாநகராாட்சி, செென்னை – 600 003
தெெரு விற்பனையாாளர்களுக்காான விதிமுறைைகள் & அறிவிக்கப்பட்ட விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடிய மண்டலங்கள் மற்றும்  
தெெரு விற்பனையாாளர்களுக்காான விதிமுறைைகள் & அறிவிக்கப்பட்ட விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடிய மண்டலங்கள் மற்றும்  
விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடாத மண்டலங்களின் பட்டியல்
விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடாத மண்டலங்களின் பட்டியல்

பிரிவு 21 இன் படி, சாலைையோ�ோர வியாாபாரிகளுக்குப் பொ�ொருந்தக்கூடிய பின்வரும் விதிமுறைைகள் தீர்மானிக்கப்பட்டுள்ளன:-
பிரிவு 21 இன் படி, சாலைையோ�ோர வியாாபாரிகளுக்குப் பொ�ொருந்தக்கூடிய பின்வரும் விதிமுறைைகள் தீர்மானிக்கப்பட்டுள்ளன:-
“21. Plan for street vending:- 
(1) Every local authority shall, in consultation with the planning authority and on the recommendations of the Town 
Vending Committee once in every five years, prepare a plan to promote the vocation of street vendors covering the 
matters contained in the First Schedule.
(2) The plan for street vending prepared by the local authority shall be submitted to the appropriate Government for 
approval and that Government shall, before notifying the plan, determine the norms applicable to the street vendors”.

அமைைப்பின் சம்பந்தப்பட்ட அதிகாாரிகளின் கவன

நிலைையங்கள் உள்ள இடங்களிலிருந்து 150 மீட்டர் தொ�ொலைைவில் சாலைையோ�ோர வியாாபாரம் செெய்யக்கூடாது

அரசு கட்டிடங்கள் உயர் நீதிமன்றம் பிற நீதிமன்றங்கள் மாவட்ட ஆட்சியர் அலுவலகம் தீயணைை
ப்பு நிலைையங்கள் 
போ�ோன்றவற்றின் நுழைைவு மற்றும் வெ�ளியே�றும் இடங்களிலிருந்து 150 மீட்டர் தொ�ொலைைவிற்குள் சாலைையோ�ோர விற்பனை 
பகுதியாாக அனுமதிக்கக்கூடாது
	
பழங்காால நினைவுச்சின்னங்கள் மற்றும் தொ�ொல்லியல் தளங்கள் மற்றும் எச்சங்கள் சட்டம், 2010 மற்றும் மாநில 
தொ�ொல்லியல் நினைவுச்சின்னங்கள் பாதுகாாப்பு சட்டம் ஆகியவற்றில் குறிப்பிடப்பட்டுள்ள பகுதிகளில் விற்பனை 
பகுதியாாக அனுமதிக்கக்கூடாது.
	
பாதுகாாப்பு கருத்தில் கொ�ொண்டு அரசு தடைைசெெய்துள்ள எந்தப் பகுதியும் சாலைையோ�ோர வியாாபாரம் செெய்ய 
அனுமதிக்கக்கூடாது
தலைைமைைப் பொ�ொறியாாளர் (பொ�ொது) அவர்களின் சுற்றறிக்கைை, த.பொ�ொ.(பொ�ொது) ந.க.எண்.அ1/366/2024, நாள் 03.12.2024ல் 
தலைைமைைப் பொ�ொறியாாளர் (பொ�ொது) அவர்களின் சுற்றறிக்கைை, த.பொ�ொ.(பொ�ொது) ந.க.எண்.அ1/366/2024, நாள் 03.12.2024ல் 
குறிப்பிடப்பட்டுள்ள நிலைையாான வழிகாாட்டி நெெறிமுறைைகள் (SOP).
குறிப்பிடப்பட்டுள்ள நிலைையாான வழிகாாட்டி நெெறிமுறைைகள் (SOP).
1.	
பெெருநகர செென்னை மாநகராாட்சி எல்லைைக்குட்பட்ட பகுதியில் உள்ள கல்வி நிறுவன
ங்களா
ான பள்ளி மற்றும் கல்லூரி 
அமைைந்துள்ள பகுதியில் 100 மீட்டர் சுற்றளவில் சாலைையோ�ோர வியாாபாரம் மே�ற்கொ�ொள்ள தடைை செெய்யப்பட்ட பகுதியாாக 
(No vending zone) நகர விற்பனைக்குழுவாால் அறிவிக்கப்பட்டுள்ளது.


18	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
2.	
காாவல் துறைை துணைை ஆணைையர் (போ�ோக்குவரத்து) அவர்களிடமிருந்து பெெறப்பட்ட No Parking என பட்டியலிடப்பட்ட 
சாலைைகள் தெெருக்கள் (எண்ணிக்கைை 22) விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடாத பகுதியாாக அறிவிக்க நகர விற்பனைக் 
குழுவினால் அனுமதிக்கப்பட்டு உள்ளது.
3.	
நகர விற்பனைக்குழுவாால் அனுமதிக்கப்பட்ட விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடிய பகுதியில் (Vending zone) பச்சைை நிற 
அறிவிப்பு பலகைை மற்றும் விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடாத பகுதிகளில் (Non vending zone) சிகப்பு நிற அறிவிப்பு 
பலகைைகள் அமைைக்க வே�ண்டும்.
4.	
அறிவிப்புப் பலகைைகள் 2 x 1 (2 அடி x 1 அடி) என்ற அளவில் தமிழ் மற்றும் ஆங்கிலம் மொ�ொழிகளில் எழுதப்பட்டிருக்க 
வே�ண்டும்.
5.	
அனைத்து மண்டலங்களிலும் நகர விற்பனைக் குழுவாால் அனுமதிக்கப்பட்ட விற்பனை செெய்யக்கூடிய பகுதிகளில் 
(Vending zone) அமைைய உள்ள சாலைையோ�ோரக் கடைைக
ளின் அளவுகள் 6x4 (6 அடி x 4 அடி) என்ற அளவில் ஒரேே 
மாதிரியாாக பச்சைை நிற வண்ணத்தில் அளவீடுகள் (Marking) செெய்ய வே�ண்டும்.
6.	
Vending zone அமைைய உள்ள சாலைையோ�ோரக்கடைைக
ளின் அளவு 6x4 (6 அடி x 4 அடி) என்ற அளவிலும் இரு 
கடைைக
ளுக்கு இடைையே�யாான இடைைவெ�ளி 2’ (2 அடி) என்ற அளவிலும் இருக்க வே�ண்டும். மே�லும் அதே� சாலைையில் 
அமைைந்துள்ள வணிக நிறுவன
ங்கள், வீடுகள் மற்றும் அலுவலகங்களுக்கு செெல்லக்கூடிய பாதைையைை தவிர்த்து 
கடைைகளைை
 அளவீடு (Marking) செெய்ய வே�ண்டும், நடைைபாதைை கடைைக
ளின் முன் வாாகன
ம் நிறுத்த அனுமதிக்காாமல் 
பாதசாரிகள் நடக்கும் விதமாக நடைைபாதைை அகலம் உறுதிசெெய்யப்பட வே�ண்டும்.
7.	
 சாலைையோ�ோரம் ஏற்கனவே� அமைைந்துள்ள நிலைையாான வணிக நிறுவன
ங்களின் ஒப்புதல் பெெற்றபின் கடைை அளவுகளைை
 
குறிக்கலாாம் (அல்லது) ஒப்புதல் பெெறமுடியாாத நிறுவன
ங்களைை
 தவிர்த்து கடைை அளவீடு செெய்யலாாம்.
